    20	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi"
    21	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi/nodeup/nodetasks"
    22	)
    23	
    24	// NvidiaBuilder installs the Nvidia driver and runtime.
    25	type NvidiaBuilder struct {
    26	        *NodeupModelContext
    27	}
    28	
    29	var _ fi.NodeupModelBuilder = &NvidiaBuilder{}
    30	
    31	// Build is responsible for installing packages.
    32	func (b *NvidiaBuilder) Build(c *fi.NodeupModelBuilderContext) error {
    33	        if b.InstallNvidiaRuntime() && b.Distribution.IsUbuntu() {
    34	                c.AddTask(&nodetasks.AptSource{
    35	                        Name:    "nvidia-container-toolkit",
    36	                        Keyring: "https://nvidia.github.io/libnvidia-container/gpgkey",
    37	                        Sources: []string{
    38	                                "deb https://nvidia.github.io/libnvidia-container/stable/deb/$(ARCH) /",
    39	                        },
    40	                })
    41	                c.AddTask(&nodetasks.Package{Name: "nvidia-container-toolkit"})
    42	                c.AddTask(&nodetasks.Package{Name: b.NodeupConfig.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage})
    43	        }
    44	        return nil
    45	}

    53	// BootstrapChannelBuilder is responsible for handling the addons in channels
    54	type BootstrapChannelBuilder struct {
    55	        *model.KopsModelContext
    56	        ClusterAddons kubemanifest.ObjectList
    57	        Lifecycle     fi.Lifecycle
    58	        templates     *templates.Templates
    59	        assetBuilder  *assets.AssetBuilder
    60	}
    61	
    62	var _ fi.CloudupModelBuilder = &BootstrapChannelBuilder{}
    63	
    64	// networkingSelector is the labels set on networking addons
    65	//
    66	// The role.kubernetes.io/networking is used to label anything related to a networking addin,
    67	// so that if we switch networking plugins (e.g. calico -> weave or vice-versa), we'll replace the
    68	// old networking plugin, and there won't be old pods "floating around".
    69	//
    70	// This means whenever we create or update a networking plugin, we should be sure that:
    71	// 1. the selector is role.kubernetes.io/networking=1
    72	// 2. every object in the manifest is labeled with role.kubernetes.io/networking=1
    73	//
    74	// TODO: Some way to test/enforce this?
    75	//
    76	// TODO: Create "empty" configurations for others, so we can delete e.g. the kopeio configuration
    77	// if we switch to kubenet?
    78	//
    79	// TODO: Create configuration object for cni providers (maybe create it but orphan it)?
    80	//
    81	// NOTE: we try to suffix with -kops.1, so that we can increment versions even if the upstream version
    82	// hasn't changed.  The problem with semver is that there is nothing > 1.0.0 other than 1.0.1-pre.1
    83	func networkingSelector() map[string]string {
    84	        return map[string]string{"role.kubernetes.io/networking": "1"}
    85	}
    86	
    87	// NewBootstrapChannelBuilder creates a new BootstrapChannelBuilder
    88	func NewBootstrapChannelBuilder(modelContext *model.KopsModelContext,
    89	        clusterLifecycle fi.Lifecycle, assetBuilder *assets.AssetBuilder,
    90	        templates *templates.Templates,
    91	        addons kubemanifest.ObjectList,
    92	) *BootstrapChannelBuilder {
    93	        return &BootstrapChannelBuilder{
    94	                KopsModelContext: modelContext,
    95	                Lifecycle:        clusterLifecycle,
    96	                assetBuilder:     assetBuilder,
    97	                templates:        templates,
    98	                ClusterAddons:    addons,
    99	        }
   100	}
   101	
   102	// Build is responsible for adding the addons to the channel
   103	func (b *BootstrapChannelBuilder) Build(c *fi.CloudupModelBuilderContext) error {
   104	        addons, serviceAccounts, err := b.buildAddons(c)
   105	        if err != nil {
   106	                return err
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        for _, a := range addons.Items {
   110	                // Older versions of channels that may be running on the upgrading cluster requires Version to be set
   111	                // We hardcode version to a high version to ensure an update is triggered on first run, and from then on
   112	                // only a hash change will trigger an addon update.
   113	                a.Spec.Version = "9.99.0"
   114	
   115	                key := *a.Spec.Name
   116	                if a.Spec.Id != "" {
   117	                        key = key + "-" + a.Spec.Id
   118	                }
   119	                name := b.Cluster.ObjectMeta.Name + "-addons-" + key
   120	                manifestPath := "addons/" + *a.Spec.Manifest
   121	                klog.V(4).Infof("Addon %q", name)
   122	
   123	                manifestResource := b.templates.Find(manifestPath)
   124	                if manifestResource == nil {
   125	                        return fmt.Errorf("unable to find manifest %s", manifestPath)
   126	                }
   127	
   128	                manifestBytes, err := fi.ResourceAsBytes(manifestResource)
   129	                if err != nil {
   130	                        return fmt.Errorf("error reading manifest %s: %v", manifestPath, err)
   131	                }
   132	
   133	                // Go through any transforms that are best expressed as code
   134	                remapped, err := addonmanifests.RemapAddonManifest(a.Spec, b.KopsModelContext, b.assetBuilder, manifestBytes, serviceAccounts)
   135	                if err != nil {
   136	                        klog.Infof("invalid manifest: %s", string(manifestBytes))
   137	                        return fmt.Errorf("error remapping manifest %s: %v", manifestPath, err)
   138	                }
   139	                manifestBytes = remapped
   140	
   141	                // Trim whitespace
   142	                manifestBytes = []byte(strings.TrimSpace(string(manifestBytes)))
   143	
   144	                a.ManifestData = manifestBytes
   145	
   146	                rawManifest := string(manifestBytes)
   147	                klog.V(4).Infof("Manifest %v", rawManifest)
   148	
   149	                manifestHash, err := utils.HashString(rawManifest)
   150	                klog.V(4).Infof("hash %s", manifestHash)
   151	                if err != nil {
   152	                        return fmt.Errorf("error hashing manifest: %v", err)
   153	                }
   154	                a.Spec.ManifestHash = manifestHash
   155	
   156	                c.AddTask(&fitasks.ManagedFile{
   157	                        Contents:  fi.NewBytesResource(manifestBytes),
   158	                        Lifecycle: b.Lifecycle,
   159	                        Location:  fi.PtrTo(manifestPath),
   160	                        Name:      fi.PtrTo(name),
   161	                })
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        if featureflag.UseAddonOperators.Enabled() {
   165	                ob := &wellknownoperators.Builder{
   166	                        VFSContext: vfs.Context,
   167	                        Cluster:    b.Cluster,
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                addonPackages, clusterAddons, err := ob.Build(b.ClusterAddons)
   171	                if err != nil {
   172	                        return fmt.Errorf("error building well-known operators: %v", err)
   173	                }
   174	                b.ClusterAddons = clusterAddons
   175	
   176	                for _, a := range addonPackages {
   177	                        key := *a.Spec.Name
   178	                        if a.Spec.Id != "" {
   179	                                key = key + "-" + a.Spec.Id
   180	                        }
   181	                        name := b.Cluster.ObjectMeta.Name + "-addons-" + key
   182	                        manifestPath := "addons/" + *a.Spec.Manifest
   183	
   184	                        // Go through any transforms that are best expressed as code
   185	                        manifestBytes, err := addonmanifests.RemapAddonManifest(&a.Spec, b.KopsModelContext, b.assetBuilder, a.Manifest, serviceAccounts)
   186	                        if err != nil {
   187	                                klog.Infof("invalid manifest: %s", string(a.Manifest))
   188	                                return fmt.Errorf("error remapping manifest %s: %v", manifestPath, err)
   189	                        }
   190	
   191	                        // Trim whitespace
   192	                        manifestBytes = []byte(strings.TrimSpace(string(manifestBytes)))
   193	
   194	                        rawManifest := string(manifestBytes)
   195	                        klog.V(4).Infof("Manifest %v", rawManifest)
   196	
   197	                        manifestHash, err := utils.HashString(rawManifest)
   198	                        klog.V(4).Infof("hash %s", manifestHash)
   199	                        if err != nil {
   200	                                return fmt.Errorf("error hashing manifest: %v", err)
   201	                        }
   202	                        a.Spec.ManifestHash = manifestHash
   203	
   204	                        c.AddTask(&fitasks.ManagedFile{
   205	                                Contents:  fi.NewBytesResource(manifestBytes),
   206	                                Lifecycle: b.Lifecycle,
   207	                                Location:  fi.PtrTo(manifestPath),
   208	                                Name:      fi.PtrTo(name),
   209	                        })
   210	
   211	                        addon := addons.Add(&a.Spec)
   212	                        addon.ManifestData = manifestBytes
   213	                }
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        // Not all objects in ClusterAddons should be applied to the cluster - although most should.
   217	        // However, there are a handful of well-known exceptions:
   218	        // e.g. configuration objects which are instead configured via files on the nodes.
   219	        var applyAdditionalObjectsToCluster kubemanifest.ObjectList
   220	        if b.ClusterAddons != nil {
   221	                for _, addon := range b.ClusterAddons {
   222	                        applyToCluster := true
   223	
   224	                        switch addon.GroupVersionKind().GroupKind() {
   225	                        case schema.GroupKind{Group: "kubescheduler.config.k8s.io", Kind: "KubeSchedulerConfiguration"}:
   226	                                applyToCluster = false
   227	                        }
   228	
   229	                        if applyToCluster {
   230	                                applyAdditionalObjectsToCluster = append(applyAdditionalObjectsToCluster, addon)
   231	                        }
   232	                }
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        if len(applyAdditionalObjectsToCluster) != 0 {
   236	                key := "cluster-addons.kops.k8s.io"
   237	                location := key + "/default.yaml"
   238	
   239	                a := &channelsapi.AddonSpec{
   240	                        Name:     fi.PtrTo(key),
   241	                        Selector: map[string]string{"k8s-addon": key},
   242	                        Manifest: fi.PtrTo(location),
   243	                }
   244	
   245	                name := b.Cluster.ObjectMeta.Name + "-addons-" + key
   246	                manifestPath := "addons/" + *a.Manifest
   247	
   248	                manifestBytes, err := applyAdditionalObjectsToCluster.ToYAML()
   249	                if err != nil {
   250	                        return fmt.Errorf("error serializing addons: %v", err)
   251	                }
   252	
   253	                // Trim whitespace
   254	                manifestBytes = []byte(strings.TrimSpace(string(manifestBytes)))
   255	
   256	                rawManifest := string(manifestBytes)
   257	
   258	                manifestHash, err := utils.HashString(rawManifest)
   259	                if err != nil {
   260	                        return fmt.Errorf("error hashing manifest: %v", err)
   261	                }
   262	                a.ManifestHash = manifestHash
   263	
   264	                c.AddTask(&fitasks.ManagedFile{
   265	                        Contents:  fi.NewBytesResource(manifestBytes),
   266	                        Lifecycle: b.Lifecycle,
   267	                        Location:  fi.PtrTo(manifestPath),
   268	                        Name:      fi.PtrTo(name),
   269	                })
   270	
   271	                addons.Add(a)
   272	        }
   273	
   274	        if err := b.addPruneDirectives(addons); err != nil {
   275	                return err
   276	        }
   277	
   278	        addonsObject := &channelsapi.Addons{}
   279	        addonsObject.Kind = "Addons"
   280	        addonsObject.ObjectMeta.Name = "bootstrap"
   281	        for _, addon := range addons.Items {
   282	                addonsObject.Spec.Addons = append(addonsObject.Spec.Addons, addon.Spec)
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        if err := addonsObject.Verify(); err != nil {
   286	                return err
   287	        }
   288	
   289	        addonsYAML, err := utils.YamlMarshal(addonsObject)
   290	        if err != nil {
   291	                return fmt.Errorf("error serializing addons yaml: %v", err)
   292	        }
   293	
   294	        name := b.Cluster.ObjectMeta.Name + "-addons-bootstrap"
   295	
   296	        c.AddTask(&fitasks.ManagedFile{
   297	                Contents:  fi.NewBytesResource(addonsYAML),
   298	                Lifecycle: b.Lifecycle,
   299	                Location:  fi.PtrTo("addons/bootstrap-channel.yaml"),
   300	                Name:      fi.PtrTo(name),
   301	        })
   302	
   303	        return nil
   304	}
   305	
   306	type AddonList struct {
   307	        Items []*Addon
   308	}
   309	
   310	func (a *AddonList) Add(spec *channelsapi.AddonSpec) *Addon {
   311	        addon := &Addon{
   312	                Spec: spec,
   313	        }
   314	        a.Items = append(a.Items, addon)
   315	        return addon
   316	}
   317	
   318	type Addon struct {
   319	        // Spec is the spec that will (eventually) be passed to the channels binary.
   320	        Spec *channelsapi.AddonSpec
   321	
   322	        // ManifestData is the object data loaded from the manifest.
   323	        ManifestData []byte
   324	
   325	        // BuildPrune is set if we should automatically build prune specifiers, based on the manifest.
   326	        BuildPrune bool
   327	}
   328	
   329	func (b *BootstrapChannelBuilder) buildAddons(c *fi.CloudupModelBuilderContext) (*AddonList, map[types.NamespacedName]iam.Subject, error) {
   330	        addons := &AddonList{}
   331	
   332	        serviceAccountRoles := []iam.Subject{}
   333	
   334	        {
   335	                key := "kops-controller.addons.k8s.io"
   336	
   337	                {
   338	                        location := key + "/k8s-1.16.yaml"
   339	                        id := "k8s-1.16"
   340	
   341	                        addons.Add(&channelsapi.AddonSpec{
   342	                                Name:               fi.PtrTo(key),
   343	                                Selector:           map[string]string{"k8s-addon": key},
   344	                                Manifest:           fi.PtrTo(location),
   345	                                NeedsRollingUpdate: channelsapi.NeedsRollingUpdateControlPlane,
   346	                                Id:                 id,

    15	#!/bin/bash
    16	set -euo pipefail
    17	set -x
    18	
    19	CACHE_DIR=/nvidia-device-plugin
    20	
    21	# Load Passthrough environment variables from the original kops hook
    22	source $CACHE_DIR/environment
    23	
    24	# Support both deviceplugin and legacy (accelerator) GPU modes.
    25	#   Default to 'deviceplugin' if env var is unset.
    26	if [[ ! -v NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE ]]; then
    27	    NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE='deviceplugin'
    28	    echo "Defaulting to NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE='deviceplugin'"
    29	fi
    30	
    31	# Figure out which scripts should run
    32	scripts=()
    33	case "$NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE" in
    34	    legacy)
    35	        scripts+=("$CACHE_DIR/01-aws-nvidia-driver.sh")
    36	        ;;
    37	    deviceplugin)
    38	        scripts+=("$CACHE_DIR/01-aws-nvidia-driver.sh")
    39	        scripts+=("$CACHE_DIR/02-nvidia-docker.sh")
    40	        ;;
    41	    *)
    42	        echo "Invalid NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE=$NVIDIA_DEVICE_PLUGIN_MODE"
    43	        echo "  Valid values are 'deviceplugin' or 'legacy'"
    44	        exit 1
    45	esac
    46	
    47	# Run the scripts
    48	for script in "${scripts[@]}"; do
    49	    echo "########## Starting $script ##########"
    50	    $script 2>&1 | tee -a $CACHE_DIR/install.log
    51	    echo "########## Finished $script ##########"
    52	done

     2	#

    11	# WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
    12	# See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
    13	# limitations under the License.
    14	
    15	#!/bin/bash
    16	set -euo pipefail
    17	set -x
    18	
    19	#################################################
    20	# Install nvidia-docker2
    21	
    22	# This section is somewhat adapted from README at:
    23	#   https://github.com/NVIDIA/nvidia-docker
    24	
    25	#######################################
    26	# Cleanup old nvidia-docker
    27	
    28	# If you have nvidia-docker 1.0 installed: we need to remove it and all existing GPU containers
    29	docker volume ls -q -f driver=nvidia-docker | xargs -r -I{} -n1 docker ps -q -a -f volume={} | xargs -r docker rm -f
    30	
    31	# Remove the old nvidia-docker if it exists
    32	apt-get purge -y nvidia-docker || true
    33	
    34	#######################################
    35	# Add package repositories
    36	
    37	# Add the package repository for docker-ce
    38	curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/debian/gpg | \
    39	  apt-key add -
    40	echo 'deb [arch=amd64] https://download.docker.com/linux/debian stretch stable' | \
    41	  tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker-ce.list
    42	
    43	# Add the package repository for nvidia-docker
    44	curl -s -L https://nvidia.github.io/nvidia-docker/gpgkey | \
    45	  apt-key add -
    46	distribution=$(. /etc/os-release;echo $ID$VERSION_ID)
    47	curl -s -L https://nvidia.github.io/nvidia-docker/$distribution/nvidia-docker.list | \
    48	  tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/nvidia-docker.list
    49	
    50	# Override the default runtime with the one from nvidia
    51	#   Also explicity set the storage-driver to the prior 'overlay'
    52	cat << 'EOF' > /etc/docker/daemon.json
    53	{
    54	    "default-runtime": "nvidia",
    55	    "runtimes": {
    56	        "nvidia": {
    57	            "path": "/usr/bin/nvidia-container-runtime",
    58	            "runtimeArgs": []
    59	        }
    60	    },
    61	    "storage-driver": "overlay"
    62	}
    63	EOF
    64	
    65	# Install nvidia-docker2 and reload the Docker daemon configuration
    66	# Note that the nvidia-docker version must match the docker-ce version
    67	# --force-confold prevents prompt for replacement of daemon.json
    68	apt-get -y update
    69	# Stop protokube to ensure not bring kubelet up again
    70	systemctl stop protokube
    71	# Stop kubelet to ensure not bring stopped containers up again and leak
    72	# them as orphan containers
    73	systemctl stop kubelet
    74	# pin versions https://github.com/NVIDIA/nvidia-docker/wiki/Frequently-Asked-Questions#how-do-i-install-20-if-im-not-using-the-latest-docker-version
    75	apt-get install -y --allow-downgrades -o Dpkg::Options::="--force-confold" \
    76	  nvidia-docker2=2.0.3+docker18.09.4-1 \
    77	  nvidia-container-runtime=2.0.0+docker18.09.4-1 \
    78	  docker-ce=5:18.09.4~3-0~debian-stretch
    79	
    80	# Disable a few things that break docker-ce/gpu support upon reboot:
    81	#  Upon boot, the kops-configuration.service systemd unit sets up and starts
    82	#  the cloud-init.service which runs nodeup which forces docker-ce to a
    83	#  specific version that is a downgrade and incompatible with nvidia-docker2.
    84	#  Permanently disable these systemd units via masking.
    85	systemctl mask cloud-init.service
    86	systemctl mask kops-configuration.service
    87	
    88	# Restore protokube and protokube will bring up kubelet
    89	systemctl start protokube
    90	# Seems protokube won't bring up kubelet, so start kubelet separately
    91	systemctl start kubelet
    92

    24	// NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage is the nvidia driver default version
    25	const NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage = "nvidia-driver-535-server"
    26	
    27	// ContainerdConfig is the configuration for containerd
    28	type ContainerdConfig struct {
    29	        // Address of containerd's GRPC server (default "/run/containerd/containerd.sock").
    30	        Address *string `json:"address,omitempty" flag:"address"`
    31	        // ConfigAdditions adds additional config entries to the generated config file.
    32	        ConfigAdditions map[string]intstr.IntOrString `json:"configAdditions,omitempty"`
    33	        // ConfigOverride is the complete containerd config file provided by the user.
    34	        ConfigOverride *string `json:"configOverride,omitempty"`
    35	        // LogLevel controls the logging details [trace, debug, info, warn, error, fatal, panic] (default "info").
    36	        LogLevel *string `json:"logLevel,omitempty" flag:"log-level"`
    37	        // Packages overrides the URL and hash for the packages.
    38	        Packages *PackagesConfig `json:"packages,omitempty"`
    39	        // RegistryMirrors is list of image registries
    40	        RegistryMirrors map[string][]string `json:"registryMirrors,omitempty"`
    41	        // Root directory for persistent data (default "/var/lib/containerd").
    42	        Root *string `json:"root,omitempty" flag:"root"`
    43	        // SkipInstall prevents kOps from installing and modifying containerd in any way (default "false").
    44	        SkipInstall bool `json:"skipInstall,omitempty"`
    45	        // State directory for execution state files (default "/run/containerd").
    46	        State *string `json:"state,omitempty" flag:"state"`
    47	        // Version used to pick the containerd package.
    48	        Version *string `json:"version,omitempty"`
    49	        // NvidiaGPU configures the Nvidia GPU runtime.
    50	        NvidiaGPU *NvidiaGPUConfig `json:"nvidiaGPU,omitempty"`
    51	        // Runc configures the runc runtime.
    52	        Runc *Runc `json:"runc,omitempty"`
    53	        // SelinuxEnabled enables SELinux support
    54	        SeLinuxEnabled bool `json:"selinuxEnabled,omitempty"`
    55	        // NRI configures the Node Resource Interface.
    56	        NRI *NRIConfig `json:"nri,omitempty"`
    57	}
    58	
    59	type NRIConfig struct {
    60	        // Enable NRI support in containerd
    61	        Enabled *bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
    62	        // PluginRegistrationTimeout is the timeout for plugin registration
    63	        PluginRegistrationTimeout *metav1.Duration `json:"pluginRegistrationTimeout,omitempty"`
    64	        // PluginRequestTimeout is the timeout for a plugin to handle a request
    65	        PluginRequestTimeout *metav1.Duration `json:"pluginRequestTimeout,omitempty"`
    66	}
    67	
    68	type NvidiaGPUConfig struct {
    69	        // Package is the name of the nvidia driver package that will be installed.
    70	        // Default is "nvidia-headless-510-server".
    71	        DriverPackage string `json:"package,omitempty"`
    72	        // Enabled determines if kOps will install the Nvidia GPU runtime and drivers.
    73	        // They will only be installed on intances that has an Nvidia GPU.
    74	        Enabled *bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
    75	        // DCGMExporterConfig configures the DCGM exporter
    76	        DCGMExporter *DCGMExporterConfig `json:"dcgmExporter,omitempty"`
    77	}
    78	
    79	// DCGMExporterConfig configures the DCGM exporter.
    80	// Only the DCGMExporterConfig in the cluster level takes effect. Configurations on the Instance Group are ignored.
    81	type DCGMExporterConfig struct {
    82	        // Enabled determines if kOps will install the DCGM exporter
    83	        Enabled bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
    84	}

    25	// ContainerdOptionsBuilder adds options for containerd to the model
    26	type ContainerdOptionsBuilder struct {
    27	        *OptionsContext
    28	}
    29	
    30	var _ loader.ClusterOptionsBuilder = &ContainerdOptionsBuilder{}
    31	
    32	// BuildOptions is responsible for filling in the default setting for containerd daemon
    33	func (b *ContainerdOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
    34	        clusterSpec := &o.Spec
    35	
    36	        if clusterSpec.Containerd == nil {
    37	                clusterSpec.Containerd = &kops.ContainerdConfig{}
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        containerd := clusterSpec.Containerd
    41	
    42	        // Set version based on Kubernetes version
    43	        if fi.ValueOf(containerd.Version) == "" {
    44	                switch {
    45	                case b.IsKubernetesLT("1.27.2"):
    46	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.6.20")
    47	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    48	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.1.5"),
    49	                        }
    50	                default:
    51	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.7.25")
    52	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    53	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.2.4"),
    54	                        }
    55	                }
    56	        }
    57	        // Set default log level to INFO
    58	        containerd.LogLevel = fi.PtrTo("info")
    59	
    60	        if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) && containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
    61	                containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return nil
    65	}

    35	// KopsAddonLabelKey is the label we use for objects in kOps manifests.
    36	// The value corresponds to the name of the addon.
    37	const KopsAddonLabelKey = "addon.kops.k8s.io/name"
    38	
    39	func RemapAddonManifest(addon *addonsapi.AddonSpec, context *model.KopsModelContext, assetBuilder *assets.AssetBuilder, manifest []byte, serviceAccounts map[types.NamespacedName]iam.Subject) ([]byte, error) {
    40	        name := fi.ValueOf(addon.Name)
    41	
    42	        {
    43	                objects, err := kubemanifest.LoadObjectsFrom(manifest)
    44	                if err != nil {
    45	                        return nil, err
    46	                }
    47	
    48	                if name == "dns-controller.addons.k8s.io" {
    49	                        if err := dnscontroller.Remap(context, addon, objects); err != nil {
    50	                                return nil, err
    51	                        }
    52	                }
    53	
    54	                err = addLabels(addon, objects)
    55	                if err != nil {
    56	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to annotate %q: %w", name, err)
    57	                }
    58	
    59	                err = addServiceAccountRole(context, objects, serviceAccounts)
    60	                if err != nil {
    61	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to add service account for %q: %w", name, err)
    62	                }
    63	
    64	                b, err := objects.ToYAML()
    65	                if err != nil {
    66	                        return nil, err
    67	                }
    68	                manifest = b
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        {
    72	                remapped, err := assetBuilder.RemapManifest(manifest)
    73	                if err != nil {
    74	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("error remapping manifest %s: %v", name, err)
    75	                }
    76	                manifest = remapped
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        return manifest, nil
    80	}
    81	
    82	func addServiceAccountRole(context *model.KopsModelContext, objects kubemanifest.ObjectList, serviceAccounts map[types.NamespacedName]iam.Subject) error {
    83	        if !context.UseServiceAccountExternalPermissions() {
    84	                return nil
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        for _, object := range objects {
    88	                if !hasPodSpecTemplate(object) {
    89	                        continue
    90	                }
    91	                podSpec := &corev1.PodSpec{}
    92	
    93	                if err := object.Reparse(podSpec, "spec", "template", "spec"); err != nil {
    94	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to parse spec.template.spec from Deployment: %v", err)
    95	                }
    96	                sa := types.NamespacedName{
    97	                        Name:      podSpec.ServiceAccountName,
    98	                        Namespace: object.GetNamespace(),
    99	                }
   100	                subject := serviceAccounts[sa]
   101	                if subject == nil {
   102	                        continue
   103	                }
   104	
   105	                if err := iam.AddServiceAccountRole(&context.IAMModelContext, podSpec, subject); err != nil {
   106	                        return err
   107	                }
   108	
   109	                if err := object.Set(podSpec, "spec", "template", "spec"); err != nil {
   110	                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to set object: %w", err)
   111	                }
   112	
   113	        }
   114	        return nil
   115	}
   116	
   117	func addLabels(addon *addonsapi.AddonSpec, objects kubemanifest.ObjectList) error {
   118	        for _, object := range objects {
   119	                meta := &metav1.ObjectMeta{}
   120	                err := object.Reparse(meta, "metadata")
   121	                if err != nil {
   122	                        return fmt.Errorf("Failed to annotate %T", object)
   123	                }
   124	
   125	                if meta.Labels == nil {
   126	                        meta.Labels = make(map[string]string)
   127	                }
   128	
   129	                meta.Labels["app.kubernetes.io/managed-by"] = "kops"
   130	                meta.Labels[KopsAddonLabelKey] = *addon.Name
   131	
   132	                // ensure selector is set where applicable
   133	                for key, val := range addon.Selector {
   134	                        existingVal, ok := meta.Labels[key]
   135	                        if ok && existingVal != val {
   136	                                return fmt.Errorf("label %q already set to %q while it should be %q", key, meta.Labels[key], val)
   137	                        }
   138	
   139	                        meta.Labels[key] = val
   140	                }
   141	                if hasPodSpecTemplate(object) {
   142	                        addPodSpecLabels(object)
   143	                }
   144	                object.Set(meta, "metadata")
   145	        }
   146	        return nil
   147	}
   148	
   149	func addPodSpecLabels(object *kubemanifest.Object) error {
   150	        podMeta := &metav1.ObjectMeta{}
   151	
   152	        if err := object.Reparse(podMeta, "spec", "template", "metadata"); err != nil {
   153	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to parse spec.template.spec from Deployment: %v", err)
   154	        }
   155	        podMeta.Labels["kops.k8s.io/managed-by"] = "kops"
   156	
   157	        if err := object.Set(podMeta, "spec", "template", "metadata"); err != nil {
   158	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to set object: %w", err)
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        return nil
   162	}
   163	
   164	func hasPodSpecTemplate(object *kubemanifest.Object) bool {
   165	        if object.Kind() == "Deployment" || object.Kind() == "DaemonSet" {
   166	                if object.APIVersion() == "apps/v1" {
   167	                        return true
   168	                }
   169	        }
   170	        return false
   171	}

    30	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi"
    31	        "k8s.io/kops/util/pkg/vfs"
    32	)
    33	
    34	type Templates struct {
    35	        cluster           *kops.Cluster
    36	        resources         map[string]fi.Resource
    37	        TemplateFunctions template.FuncMap
    38	}
    39	
    40	func LoadTemplates(ctx context.Context, cluster *kops.Cluster, base vfs.Path) (*Templates, error) {
    41	        t := &Templates{
    42	                cluster:           cluster,
    43	                resources:         make(map[string]fi.Resource),
    44	                TemplateFunctions: make(template.FuncMap),
    45	        }
    46	        err := t.loadFrom(ctx, base)
    47	        if err != nil {
    48	                return nil, err
    49	        }
    50	        return t, nil
    51	}
    52	
    53	func (t *Templates) Find(key string) fi.Resource {
    54	        return t.resources[key]
    55	}
    56	
    57	func (t *Templates) loadFrom(ctx context.Context, base vfs.Path) error {
    58	        files, err := base.ReadTree(ctx)
    59	        if err != nil {
    60	                return fmt.Errorf("error reading from %s", base)
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        for _, f := range files {
    64	                contents, err := f.ReadFile(ctx)
    65	                if err != nil {
    66	                        if os.IsNotExist(err) {
    67	                                // This is just an annoyance of gobindata - we can't tell the difference between files & directories.  Ignore.
    68	                                continue
    69	                        }
    70	                        return fmt.Errorf("error reading %s: %v", f, err)
    71	                }
    72	
    73	                key, err := vfs.RelativePath(base, f)
    74	                if err != nil {
    75	                        return fmt.Errorf("error getting relative path for %s", f)
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                var resource fi.Resource
    79	                if strings.HasSuffix(key, ".template") {
    80	                        key = strings.TrimSuffix(key, ".template")
    81	                        klog.V(6).Infof("loading (templated) resource %q", key)
    82	
    83	                        resource = &templateResource{
    84	                                template: string(contents),
    85	                                loader:   t,
    86	                                key:      key,
    87	                        }
    88	                } else {
    89	                        klog.V(6).Infof("loading resource %q", key)
    90	                        resource = fi.NewBytesResource(contents)
    91	
    92	                }
    93	
    94	                t.resources[key] = resource
    95	        }
    96	        return nil
    97	}
    98

   100	        t := template.New(key)

    99	func (l *Templates) executeTemplate(key string, d string) (string, error) {
   100	        t := template.New(key)
   101	
   102	        funcMap := make(template.FuncMap)
   103	        //funcMap["Args"] = func() []string {
   104	        //      return args
   105	        //}
   106	        //funcMap["RenderResource"] = func(resourceName string, args []string) (string, error) {
   107	        //      return l.renderResource(resourceName, args)
   108	        //}
   109	        for k, fn := range l.TemplateFunctions {
   110	                funcMap[k] = fn
   111	        }
   112	        t.Funcs(funcMap)
   113	
   114	        t.Option("missingkey=zero")
   115	
   116	        spec := l.cluster.Spec
   117	
   118	        _, err := t.Parse(d)
   119	        if err != nil {
   120	                return "", fmt.Errorf("error parsing template %q: %v", key, err)
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        var buffer bytes.Buffer
   124	        err = t.ExecuteTemplate(&buffer, key, spec)
   125	        if err != nil {
   126	                return "", fmt.Errorf("error executing template %q: %v", key, err)
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        return buffer.String(), nil
   130	}
   131	
   132	type templateResource struct {
   133	        key      string
   134	        loader   *Templates
   135	        template string
   136	}
   137	
   138	var _ fi.Resource = &templateResource{}
   139	
   140	func (a *templateResource) Open() (io.Reader, error) {
   141	        var err error
   142	        result, err := a.loader.executeTemplate(a.key, a.template)
   143	        if err != nil {
   144	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error executing resource template %q: %v", a.key, err)
   145	        }
   146	        reader := bytes.NewReader([]byte(result))
   147	        return reader, nil
   148	}

    24	// ContainerdConfig is the configuration for containerd
    25	type ContainerdConfig struct {
    26	        // Address of containerd's GRPC server (default "/run/containerd/containerd.sock").
    27	        Address *string `json:"address,omitempty" flag:"address"`
    28	        // ConfigAdditions adds additional config entries to the generated config file.
    29	        ConfigAdditions map[string]intstr.IntOrString `json:"configAdditions,omitempty"`
    30	        // ConfigOverride is the complete containerd config file provided by the user.
    31	        ConfigOverride *string `json:"configOverride,omitempty"`
    32	        // LogLevel controls the logging details [trace, debug, info, warn, error, fatal, panic] (default "info").
    33	        LogLevel *string `json:"logLevel,omitempty" flag:"log-level"`
    34	        // Packages overrides the URL and hash for the packages.
    35	        Packages *PackagesConfig `json:"packages,omitempty"`
    36	        // RegistryMirrors is list of image registries
    37	        RegistryMirrors map[string][]string `json:"registryMirrors,omitempty"`
    38	        // Root directory for persistent data (default "/var/lib/containerd").
    39	        Root *string `json:"root,omitempty" flag:"root"`
    40	        // SkipInstall prevents kOps from installing and modifying containerd in any way (default "false").
    41	        SkipInstall bool `json:"skipInstall,omitempty"`
    42	        // State directory for execution state files (default "/run/containerd").
    43	        State *string `json:"state,omitempty" flag:"state"`
    44	        // Version used to pick the containerd package.
    45	        Version *string `json:"version,omitempty"`
    46	        // NvidiaGPU configures the Nvidia GPU runtime.
    47	        NvidiaGPU *NvidiaGPUConfig `json:"nvidiaGPU,omitempty"`
    48	        // Runc configures the runc runtime.
    49	        Runc *Runc `json:"runc,omitempty"`
    50	        // SelinuxEnabled enables SELinux support
    51	        SeLinuxEnabled bool `json:"selinuxEnabled,omitempty"`
    52	        // NRI configures the Node Resource Interface.
    53	        NRI *NRIConfig `json:"nri,omitempty"`
    54	}
    55	
    56	type NRIConfig struct {
    57	        // Enable NRI support in containerd
    58	        Enabled *bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
    59	        // PluginRegistrationTimeout is the timeout for plugin registration
    60	        PluginRegistrationTimeout *metav1.Duration `json:"pluginRegistrationTimeout,omitempty"`
    61	        // PluginRequestTimeout is the timeout for a plugin to handle a request
    62	        PluginRequestTimeout *metav1.Duration `json:"pluginRequestTimeout,omitempty"`
    63	}
    64	
    65	type NvidiaGPUConfig struct {
    66	        // Package is the name of the nvidia driver package that will be installed.
    67	        // Default is "nvidia-headless-460-server".
    68	        DriverPackage string `json:"package,omitempty"`
    69	        // Enabled determines if kOps will install the Nvidia GPU runtime and drivers.
    70	        // They will only be installed on intances that has an Nvidia GPU.
    71	        Enabled *bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
    72	        // DCGMExporterConfig configures the DCGM exporter
    73	        DCGMExporter *DCGMExporterConfig `json:"dcgmExporter,omitempty"`
    74	}
    75	
    76	// DCGMExporterConfig configures the DCGM exporter.
    77	// Only the DCGMExporterConfig in the cluster level takes effect. Configurations on the Instance Group are ignored.
    78	type DCGMExporterConfig struct {
    79	        // Enabled determines if kOps will install the DCGM exporter
    80	        Enabled bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
    81	}
    82	
    83	type Runc struct {
    84	        // Version used to pick the runc package.
    85	        Version *string `json:"version,omitempty"`
    86	        // Packages overrides the URL and hash for the packages.
    87	        Packages *PackagesConfig `json:"packages,omitempty"`
    88	}

    25	// ContainerdOptionsBuilder adds options for containerd to the model

    27	        *OptionsContext
    28	}
    29

    31	
    32	// BuildOptions is responsible for filling in the default setting for containerd daemon
    33	func (b *ContainerdOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
    34	        clusterSpec := &o.Spec
    35	
    36	        if clusterSpec.Containerd == nil {
    37	                clusterSpec.Containerd = &kops.ContainerdConfig{}
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        containerd := clusterSpec.Containerd
    41	
    42	        // Set version based on Kubernetes version
    43	        if fi.ValueOf(containerd.Version) == "" {
    44	                switch {
    45	                case b.IsKubernetesLT("1.27.2"):
    46	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.6.20")
    47	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    48	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.1.5"),
    49	                        }
    50	                default:
    51	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.7.25")
    52	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    53	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.2.4"),
    54	                        }
    55	                }
    56	        }
    57	        // Set default log level to INFO
    58	        containerd.LogLevel = fi.PtrTo("info")
    59	
    60	        if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) && containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
    61	                containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        return nil
    65	}

old_text = '''	if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) && containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
		containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
	}

	return nil'''

new_text = '''	if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
		if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
			containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
		}
		if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion == nil {
			containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion = fi.PtrTo(kops.NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion)
		}
	}

	return nil'''

content = content.replace(old_text, new_text)

with open('/testbed/pkg/model/components/containerd.go', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
print("Done!")
ENDPY

/*
Copyright 2019 The Kubernetes Authors.

Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
You may obtain a copy of the License at

    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0

Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
limitations under the License.

package components

import (
	"k8s.io/kops/pkg/apis/kops"
	"k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi"
	"k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi/loader"
)

// ContainerdOptionsBuilder adds options for containerd to the model
type ContainerdOptionsBuilder struct {
	*OptionsContext
}

var _ loader.ClusterOptionsBuilder = &ContainerdOptionsBuilder{}

// BuildOptions is responsible for filling in the default setting for containerd daemon
func (b *ContainerdOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
	clusterSpec := &o.Spec

	if clusterSpec.Containerd == nil {
		clusterSpec.Containerd = &kops.ContainerdConfig{}
	}

	containerd := clusterSpec.Containerd

	// Set version based on Kubernetes version
	if fi.ValueOf(containerd.Version) == "" {
		switch {
		case b.IsKubernetesLT("1.27.2"):
			containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.6.20")
			containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
				Version: fi.PtrTo("1.1.5"),
			}
		default:
			containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.7.25")
			containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
				Version: fi.PtrTo("1.2.4"),
			}
		}
	}
	// Set default log level to INFO
	containerd.LogLevel = fi.PtrTo("info")

	if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
		if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
			containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
		}
		if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion == nil {
			containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion = fi.PtrTo(kops.NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion)
		}
	}

	return nil
}
ENDFILE

    25	// ContainerdOptionsBuilder adds options for containerd to the model
    26	type ContainerdOptionsBuilder struct {
    27	*OptionsContext
    28	}
    29	
    30	var _ loader.ClusterOptionsBuilder = &ContainerdOptionsBuilder{}
    31	
    32	// BuildOptions is responsible for filling in the default setting for containerd daemon
    33	func (b *ContainerdOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
    34	clusterSpec := &o.Spec
    35	
    36	if clusterSpec.Containerd == nil {
    37	clusterSpec.Containerd = &kops.ContainerdConfig{}
    38	}
    39	
    40	containerd := clusterSpec.Containerd
    41	
    42	// Set version based on Kubernetes version
    43	if fi.ValueOf(containerd.Version) == "" {
    44	switch {
    45	case b.IsKubernetesLT("1.27.2"):
    46	containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.6.20")
    47	containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    48	Version: fi.PtrTo("1.1.5"),
    49	}
    50	default:
    51	containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.7.25")
    52	containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    53	Version: fi.PtrTo("1.2.4"),
    54	}
    55	}
    56	}
    57	// Set default log level to INFO
    58	containerd.LogLevel = fi.PtrTo("info")
    59	
    60	if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
    61	if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
    62	containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
    63	}
    64	if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion == nil {
    65	containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion = fi.PtrTo(kops.NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion)
    66	}
    67	}
    68	
    69	return nil
    70	}

    19	import (
    20	        "k8s.io/kops/pkg/apis/kops"
    21	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi"
    22	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi/loader"
    23	)
    24	
    25	// ContainerdOptionsBuilder adds options for containerd to the model
    26	type ContainerdOptionsBuilder struct {
    27	        *OptionsContext
    28	}
    29	
    30	var _ loader.ClusterOptionsBuilder = &ContainerdOptionsBuilder{}
    31	
    32	// BuildOptions is responsible for filling in the default setting for containerd daemon
    33	func (b *ContainerdOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
    34	        clusterSpec := &o.Spec
    35	
    36	        if clusterSpec.Containerd == nil {
    37	                clusterSpec.Containerd = &kops.ContainerdConfig{}
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        containerd := clusterSpec.Containerd
    41	
    42	        // Set version based on Kubernetes version
    43	        if fi.ValueOf(containerd.Version) == "" {
    44	                switch {
    45	                case b.IsKubernetesLT("1.27.2"):
    46	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.6.20")
    47	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    48	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.1.5"),
    49	                        }
    50	                default:
    51	                        containerd.Version = fi.PtrTo("1.7.25")
    52	                        containerd.Runc = &kops.Runc{
    53	                                Version: fi.PtrTo("1.2.4"),
    54	                        }
    55	                }
    56	        }
    57	        // Set default log level to INFO
    58	        containerd.LogLevel = fi.PtrTo("info")
    59	
    60	        if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
    61	                if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
    62	                        containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
    63	                }
    64	                if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion == nil {
    65	                        containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion = fi.PtrTo(kops.NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion)
    66	                }
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        return nil
    70	}

func (in *NvidiaGPUConfig) DeepCopyInto(out *NvidiaGPUConfig) {
	*out = *in
	if in.Enabled != nil {
		in, out := &in.Enabled, &out.Enabled
		*out = new(bool)
		**out = **in
	}
	if in.DCGMExporter != nil {
		in, out := &in.DCGMExporter, &out.DCGMExporter
		*out = new(DCGMExporterConfig)
		**out = **in
	}
	return
}

#!/usr/bin/env python3

file_path = '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/zz_generated.deepcopy.go'
with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Find and replace the NvidiaGPUConfig DeepCopyInto function
old_text = '''func (in *NvidiaGPUConfig) DeepCopyInto(out *NvidiaGPUConfig) {
	*out = *in
	if in.Enabled != nil {
		in, out := &in.Enabled, &out.Enabled
		*out = new(bool)
		**out = **in
	}
	if in.DCGMExporter != nil {
		in, out := &in.DCGMExporter, &out.DCGMExporter
		*out = new(DCGMExporterConfig)
		**out = **in
	}
	return
}'''

new_text = '''func (in *NvidiaGPUConfig) DeepCopyInto(out *NvidiaGPUConfig) {
	*out = *in
	if in.Enabled != nil {
		in, out := &in.Enabled, &out.Enabled
		*out = new(bool)
		**out = **in
	}
	if in.DCGMExporter != nil {
		in, out := &in.DCGMExporter, &out.DCGMExporter
		*out = new(DCGMExporterConfig)
		**out = **in
	}
	if in.DevicePluginVersion != nil {
		in, out := &in.DevicePluginVersion, &out.DevicePluginVersion
		*out = new(string)
		**out = **in
	}
	return
}'''

content = content.replace(old_text, new_text)

with open(file_path, 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)
    
print("Updated /testbed/pkg/apis/kops/zz_generated.deepcopy.go")
ENDPY

func autoConvert_v1alpha2_NvidiaGPUConfig_To_kops_NvidiaGPUConfig(in *NvidiaGPUConfig, out *kops.NvidiaGPUConfig, s conversion.Scope) error {
	out.DriverPackage = in.DriverPackage
	out.Enabled = in.Enabled
	if in.DCGMExporter != nil {
		in, out := &in.DCGMExporter, &out.DCGMExporter
		*out = new(kops.DCGMExporterConfig)

"""
Test script to verify the NVIDIA device plugin version configuration
"""
import yaml
import subprocess
import sys

def test_template_rendering():
    """Test that the template can use the DevicePluginVersion field"""
    
    # Create a test input file with the device plugin version
    test_yaml = """
apiVersion: kops.k8s.io/v1alpha2
kind: Cluster
metadata:
  name: test.k8s.local
spec:
  kubernetesVersion: v1.28.0
  containerd:
    nvidiaGPU:
      enabled: true
      devicePluginVersion: v0.15.0
  networkCIDR: 10.0.0.0/16
  nonMasqueradeCIDR: 100.64.0.0/10
  subnets:
  - cidr: 10.0.1.0/24
    name: us-test-1a
    type: Public
    zone: us-test-1a
"""
    
    print("Test YAML:")
    print(test_yaml)
    print()
    
    # Write test input
    with open('"'"'/tmp/test_cluster.yaml'"'"', '"'"'w'"'"') as f:
        f.write(test_yaml)
    
    print("✓ Test input created successfully")
    
    # Check that our API fields are present
    print("\n=== Checking API Files ===")
    check_files = [
        '"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/containerdconfig.go'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/containerdconfig.go'"'"',
    ]
    
    for filepath in check_files:
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if '"'"'DevicePluginVersion'"'"' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} contains DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion")
            return False
    
    # Check constants
    with open('"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if '"'"'NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion'"'"' in content:
        print("✓ NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion constant exists")
    else:
        print("✗ NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion constant missing")
        return False
    
    # Check component builder
    with open('"'"'/testbed/pkg/model/components/containerd.go'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if '"'"'DevicePluginVersion'"'"' in content:
        print("✓ Component builder sets DevicePluginVersion")
    else:
        print("✗ Component builder missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    # Check template
    with open('"'"'/testbed/upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if '"'"'DevicePluginVersion'"'"' in content or '"'"'devicePluginVersion'"'"' in content:
        print("✓ Template uses DevicePluginVersion")
        # Extract the line with the image
        for line in content.split('"'"'\n'"'"'):
            if '"'"'k8s-device-plugin'"'"' in line and '"'"'image:'"'"' in line:
                print(f"  Image line: {line.strip()}")
    else:
        print("✗ Template missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    print("\n=== All checks passed! ===")
    return True

if __name__ == "__main__":
    success = test_template_rendering()
    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test script to verify the NVIDIA device plugin version configuration
"""
import sys

def test_files():
    """Test that all necessary files have been updated"""
    
    print("=== Checking API Files ===")
    check_files = [
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/containerdconfig.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/containerdconfig.go',
    ]
    
    for filepath in check_files:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if 'DevicePluginVersion' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} contains DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion")
            return False
    
    # Check constants
    with open('/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go', 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if 'NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion' in content:
        print("✓ NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion constant exists")
        # Find the value
        for line in content.split('\n'):
            if 'NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion' in line and '=' in line:
                print(f"  Value: {line.strip()}")
    else:
        print("✗ NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion constant missing")
        return False
    
    # Check component builder
    with open('/testbed/pkg/model/components/containerd.go', 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if 'DevicePluginVersion' in content:
        print("✓ Component builder sets DevicePluginVersion")
    else:
        print("✗ Component builder missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    # Check template
    with open('/testbed/upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template', 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if '.Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion' in content:
        print("✓ Template uses DevicePluginVersion")
        # Extract the line with the image
        for line in content.split('\n'):
            if 'k8s-device-plugin' in line and 'image:' in line:
                print(f"  Image line: {line.strip()}")
    else:
        print("✗ Template missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    # Check deepcopy files
    print("\n=== Checking DeepCopy Files ===")
    deepcopy_files = [
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/zz_generated.deepcopy.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/zz_generated.deepcopy.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/zz_generated.deepcopy.go',
    ]
    
    for filepath in deepcopy_files:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if 'in.DevicePluginVersion' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} handles DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion handling")
            return False
    
    # Check conversion files
    print("\n=== Checking Conversion Files ===")
    conversion_files = [
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/zz_generated.conversion.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/zz_generated.conversion.go',
    ]
    
    for filepath in conversion_files:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if 'out.DevicePluginVersion = in.DevicePluginVersion' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} converts DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion conversion")
            return False
    
    print("\n=== All checks passed! ===")
    return True

if __name__ == "__main__":
    success = test_files()
    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test script to verify the NVIDIA device plugin version configuration
"""
import sys

def test_files():
    """Test that all necessary files have been updated"""
    
    print("=== Checking API Files ===")
    check_files = [
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/containerdconfig.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/containerdconfig.go',
    ]
    
    for filepath in check_files:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if 'DevicePluginVersion' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} contains DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion")
            return False
    
    # Check constants
    with open('/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go', 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if 'NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion' in content:
        print("✓ NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion constant exists")
        # Find the value
        for line in content.split('\n'):
            if 'NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion' in line and '=' in line:
                print(f"  Value: {line.strip()}")
    else:
        print("✗ NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion constant missing")
        return False
    
    # Check component builder
    with open('/testbed/pkg/model/components/containerd.go', 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if 'DevicePluginVersion' in content:
        print("✓ Component builder sets DevicePluginVersion")
    else:
        print("✗ Component builder missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    # Check template
    with open('/testbed/upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template', 'r') as f:
        content = f.read()
    if '.Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion' in content:
        print("✓ Template uses DevicePluginVersion")
        # Extract the line with the image
        for line in content.split('\n'):
            if 'k8s-device-plugin' in line and 'image:' in line:
                print(f"  Image line: {line.strip()}")
    else:
        print("✗ Template missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    # Check deepcopy files
    print("\n=== Checking DeepCopy Files ===")
    deepcopy_files = [
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/zz_generated.deepcopy.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/zz_generated.deepcopy.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/zz_generated.deepcopy.go',
    ]
    
    for filepath in deepcopy_files:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if 'in.DevicePluginVersion' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} handles DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion handling")
            return False
    
    # Check conversion files
    print("\n=== Checking Conversion Files ===")
    conversion_files = [
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/zz_generated.conversion.go',
        '/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/zz_generated.conversion.go',
    ]
    
    for filepath in conversion_files:
        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if 'out.DevicePluginVersion = in.DevicePluginVersion' in content:
            print(f"✓ {filepath} converts DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {filepath} missing DevicePluginVersion conversion")
            return False
    
    print("\n=== All checks passed! ===")
    return True

if __name__ == "__main__":
    success = test_files()
    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)

import sys

def test_complete_implementation():

        print("✓ Main API (kops) has DevicePluginVersion field")
    else:
        print("✗ Main API missing DevicePluginVersion")
        return False

        print("✓ Default version constant is v0.17.0")
    else:
        print("✗ Default version constant incorrect")
        return False

        if '"'"'DevicePluginVersion *string'"'"' in f.read():
            print("✓ v1alpha2 API has DevicePluginVersion field")
        else:
            print("✗ v1alpha2 API missing DevicePluginVersion")
            return False

    with open('"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/containerdconfig.go'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        if '"'"'DevicePluginVersion *string'"'"' in f.read():
            print("✓ v1alpha3 API has DevicePluginVersion field")
        else:
            print("✗ v1alpha3 API missing DevicePluginVersion")
            return False
    
    # Test 2: Component Builder
    print("\n[TEST 2] Component Builder")
    print("-" * 70)
    
    with open('"'"'/testbed/pkg/model/components/containerd.go'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    if '"'"'containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion = fi.PtrTo(kops.NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion)'"'"' in content:
        print("✓ Component builder sets default DevicePluginVersion")
    else:
        print("✗ Component builder doesn'"'"'t set DevicePluginVersion")
        return False
    
    # Test 3: Template
    print("\n[TEST 3] Template")
    print("-" * 70)
    
    with open('"'"'/testbed/upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()

        print("✗ Template still has hardcoded v0.12.2")
        return False
    else:
        print("✓ Template no longer has hardcoded v0.12.2")
    
    # Check that template uses the variable
    if '"'"'{{ with .Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion }}{{ . }}{{ else }}v0.17.0{{ end }}'"'"' in content:
        print("✓ Template uses DevicePluginVersion with v0.17.0 fallback")
    else:
        print("✗ Template doesn'"'"'t use DevicePluginVersion correctly")
        return False
    
    # Extract and show the image line
    for line in content.split('"'"'\n'"'"'):
        if '"'"'image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin'"'"' in line:
            print(f"  Image line: {line.strip()}")
    
    # Test 4: DeepCopy Functions
    print("\n[TEST 4] DeepCopy Functions")
    print("-" * 70)
    
    deepcopy_files = {
        '"'"'kops'"'"': '"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/zz_generated.deepcopy.go'"'"',
        '"'"'v1alpha2'"'"': '"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha2/zz_generated.deepcopy.go'"'"',
        '"'"'v1alpha3'"'"': '"'"'/testbed/pkg/apis/kops/v1alpha3/zz_generated.deepcopy.go'"'"',
    }
    
    for name, filepath in deepcopy_files.items():
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
        if '"'"'if in.DevicePluginVersion != nil'"'"' in content and '"'"'**out = **in'"'"' in content:
            print(f"✓ {name} deepcopy handles DevicePluginVersion")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {name} deepcopy missing DevicePluginVersion")
            return False

    print("\n[TEST 5] Conversion Functions")

            return False

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /tmp/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md --file_text '# NVIDIA K8s Device Plugin Version Configuration

## Summary

This implementation adds support for configuring the NVIDIA k8s-device-plugin version in kOps, addressing the issue where the version was hardcoded to v0.12.2 (now updated to v0.17.0 by default).

## Problem Statement

As described in the PR:
- The NVIDIA k8s-device-plugin version was hardcoded in kOps 
- The latest version available is v0.17.2, but kOps was using v0.12.2
- Users couldn'"'"'t override the version or configure timeSlicing features
- Manual patching of the DaemonSet would be overridden by `kops update`

## Solution

Added a new `devicePluginVersion` field to the `NvidiaGPUConfig` structure that allows users to specify which version of the NVIDIA device plugin to use.

## Changes Made

### 1. API Changes (`pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go`)
- Added `DevicePluginVersion *string` field to `NvidiaGPUConfig` struct
- Added constant `NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion = "v0.17.0"`
- Updated default from v0.12.2 to v0.17.0

### 2. Component Builder (`pkg/model/components/containerd.go`)
- Updated `BuildOptions()` to set default `DevicePluginVersion` when not specified
- Ensures backward compatibility by providing a sensible default

### 3. Template (`upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template`)
- Changed hardcoded image version from:
  ```yaml
  image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:v0.12.2
  ```
  To dynamic version:
  ```yaml
  image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:{{ with .Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion }}{{ . }}{{ else }}v0.17.0{{ end }}
  ```

### 4. Generated Code
- Updated `zz_generated.deepcopy.go` files for kops, v1alpha2, and v1alpha3
- Updated `zz_generated.conversion.go` files for v1alpha2 and v1alpha3
- Ensures proper serialization, deserialization, and version conversion

## Usage

Users can now configure the device plugin version in their cluster spec:

```yaml
apiVersion: kops.k8s.io/v1alpha2
kind: Cluster
metadata:
  name: my-cluster.example.com
spec:
  containerd:
    nvidiaGPU:
      enabled: true
      devicePluginVersion: v0.17.2  # Specify desired version
```

If `devicePluginVersion` is not specified, it defaults to v0.17.0.

## Benefits

1. **Version Control**: Users can specify exact versions of the device plugin
2. **Up-to-date Defaults**: Default version updated from v0.12.2 to v0.17.0
3. **Feature Access**: Newer versions support features like GPU timeSlicing
4. **Flexibility**: Easy to rollback to older versions if needed
5. **No Manual Patching**: Changes persist through `kops update`

## Testing

Run the test script to verify all changes:
```bash
python3 /tmp/test_nvidia_complete.py
```

## Examples

See `/tmp/example_usage.yaml` for complete examples including:
- Default version usage
- Custom version specification  
- Legacy version for compatibility
- Full configuration with DCGM exporter

## Backward Compatibility

- Existing clusters without `devicePluginVersion` specified will automatically use v0.17.0
- The field is optional with a sensible default
- All v1alpha2 and v1alpha3 APIs are updated for consistency

## Related Links

- Original Issue: https://github.com/kubernetes/kops/issues/14103
- NVIDIA Device Plugin: https://github.com/NVIDIA/k8s-device-plugin
- TimeSlicing Documentation: https://github.com/NVIDIA/k8s-device-plugin?tab=readme-ov-file#shared-access-to-gpus

# NVIDIA K8s Device Plugin Version Configuration

## Summary

This implementation adds support for configuring the NVIDIA k8s-device-plugin version in kOps, addressing the issue where the version was hardcoded to v0.12.2 (now updated to v0.17.0 by default).

## Problem Statement

As described in the PR:
- The NVIDIA k8s-device-plugin version was hardcoded in kOps 
- The latest version available is v0.17.2, but kOps was using v0.12.2
- Users couldn't override the version or configure timeSlicing features
- Manual patching of the DaemonSet would be overridden by `kops update`

## Solution

Added a new `devicePluginVersion` field to the `NvidiaGPUConfig` structure that allows users to specify which version of the NVIDIA device plugin to use.

## Changes Made

### 1. API Changes (`pkg/apis/kops/containerdconfig.go`)
- Added `DevicePluginVersion *string` field to `NvidiaGPUConfig` struct
- Added constant `NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion = "v0.17.0"`
- Updated default from v0.12.2 to v0.17.0

### 2. Component Builder (`pkg/model/components/containerd.go`)
- Updated `BuildOptions()` to set default `DevicePluginVersion` when not specified
- Ensures backward compatibility by providing a sensible default

### 3. Template (`upup/models/cloudup/resources/addons/nvidia.addons.k8s.io/k8s-1.16.yaml.template`)
- Changed hardcoded image version from:
  ```yaml
  image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:v0.12.2
  ```
  To dynamic version:
  ```yaml
  image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:{{ with .Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion }}{{ . }}{{ else }}v0.17.0{{ end }}
  ```

### 4. Generated Code
- Updated `zz_generated.deepcopy.go` files for kops, v1alpha2, and v1alpha3
- Updated `zz_generated.conversion.go` files for v1alpha2 and v1alpha3
- Ensures proper serialization, deserialization, and version conversion

## Usage

Users can now configure the device plugin version in their cluster spec:

```yaml
apiVersion: kops.k8s.io/v1alpha2
kind: Cluster
metadata:
  name: my-cluster.example.com
spec:
  containerd:
    nvidiaGPU:
      enabled: true
      devicePluginVersion: v0.17.2  # Specify desired version
```

## Benefits

NVIDIA K8s Device Plugin Version Configuration - Demonstration

[1] API Structure - NvidiaGPUConfig
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
type NvidiaGPUConfig struct {
	// Package is the name of the nvidia driver package that will be installed.
	// Default is "nvidia-headless-510-server".
	DriverPackage string `json:"package,omitempty"`
	// Enabled determines if kOps will install the Nvidia GPU runtime and drivers.
	// They will only be installed on intances that has an Nvidia GPU.
	Enabled *bool `json:"enabled,omitempty"`
	// DCGMExporterConfig configures the DCGM exporter
	DCGMExporter *DCGMExporterConfig `json:"dcgmExporter,omitempty"`
	// DevicePluginVersion is the version of the Nvidia device plugin to install.
	// Default is determined by the component builder.
	DevicePluginVersion *string `json:"devicePluginVersion,omitempty"`
}

[2] Default Version Constant
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion is the nvidia device plugin default version
const NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion = "v0.17.0"

[3] Component Builder Setting Default
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	if containerd.NvidiaGPU != nil && fi.ValueOf(containerd.NvidiaGPU.Enabled) {
		if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage == "" {
			containerd.NvidiaGPU.DriverPackage = kops.NvidiaDefaultDriverPackage
		}
		if containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion == nil {
			containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion = fi.PtrTo(kops.NvidiaDefaultDevicePluginVersion)
		}
	}

	return nil
}

[4] Template Using the Field
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      - image: nvcr.io/nvidia/k8s-device-plugin:{{ with .Containerd.NvidiaGPU.DevicePluginVersion }}{{ . }}{{ else }}v0.17.0{{ end }}

[5] Example Usage
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Minimal configuration - uses default v0.17.0
spec:
  containerd:
    nvidiaGPU:
      enabled: true

# Custom version - uses specified version
spec:
  containerd:
    nvidiaGPU:
      enabled: true
      devicePluginVersion: v0.17.2


[6] Benefits
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

✓ Backward compatible with sensible default
✓ Changes persist through 'kops update'
